C
C  Cross sections for ionization of K, L and M shells of atoms by
C  impact of electrons and positrons with kinetic energies up to 1 GeV.
C  Analytical formulas.
C
C  The external functions XIONE and XIONP are standalone.
C
C  D. Bote, F. Salvat, A. Jablonski and C.J. Powell (November 2008)
C
      IMPLICIT DOUBLE PRECISION (A-H,O-Z), INTEGER*4 (I-N)
      CHARACTER*25 OFILE
C
C  ****  Generate a file with the x section table.
C
      WRITE(6,*) 'Atomic number?'
      READ(5,*) IZ
      WRITE(6,'(1X, ''Atomic number ='',I3)') IZ
      IF(IZ.LT.1.OR.IZ.GT.99)
     1   STOP 'IZ can only take values from 1 to 99.'
      WRITE(6,*) 'Enter the shell number (1 to 9, inclusive)'
      READ(5,*) ISH
      WRITE(6,'(1X, ''Active shell  ='',I3)') ISH
      WRITE(6,*) 'Type the name of the output file. (Maximum 25'
     1  ,' characters)'
      READ(5,'(A25)') OFILE
C
      OPEN(21,FILE=OFILE)
      WRITE(21,'(''# Atomic number = '',I2,'', shell = '',I2)') IZ,ISH
      WRITE(21,'(''#               electron     positron  '')')
      WRITE(21,'(''#   Energy      x section    x section '')')
      WRITE(21,'(''#    (eV)        (cm**2)      (cm**2)  '')')
      WRITE(21,'(''#--------------------------------------'')')
C
      FACT=10.0D0**(1.0D0/DBLE(80))
      EEV=10.0D0/FACT
      DO I=1,641
        EEV=EEV*FACT
        XSE=XIONE(EEV,IZ,ISH)
        XSP=XIONP(EEV,IZ,ISH)
        WRITE(21,'(1P,3E13.5)') EEV,XSE,XSP
        WRITE( 6,'(1P,3E13.5)') EEV,XSE,XSP
      ENDDO
C
      CLOSE(21)
      END
C  *********************************************************************
C                       FUNCION XIONE
C  *********************************************************************
      FUNCTION XIONE(EEV,IZ,ISH)
C
C     This function delivers the total cross section for electron impact
C  ionization of K, L and M shells of neutral atoms of the elements from
C  hydrogen (IZ=1) to einsteinium (IZ=99). It uses a parameterization of
C  numerical cross sections computed with the distorted-wave and the
C  plane-wave first-Born approximations.
C
C  References:
C  - D. Bote and F. Salvat, "Calculations of inner-shell ionization by
C       electron impact with the distorted-wave and plane-wave Born
C       approximations", Phys. Rev. A77, 042701 (2008).
C  - D. Bote et al., "Cross sections for ionization of K, L and M shells
C       of atoms by impact of electrons and positrons with energies up
C       to 1 GeV. Analytical formulas", At. and Nucl. Data Tables
C       95(6), 871--909 (2009).
C
C  Input Arguments:
C     EEV ..... kinetic energy of the projectile electron (in eV).
C     IZ ...... atomic number of the target atom (IZ=1 to 99).
C     ISH ..... active target electron shell,
C                1=K, 2=L1, 3=L2, 4=L3, 5=M1, ..., 9=M5.
C
C  Output value:
C     XIONE ... ionization cross section (in cm**2) of the ISH shell.
C
C  D. Bote, F. Salvat, A. Jablonski and C.J. Powell (November 2008)
C
      IMPLICIT DOUBLE PRECISION (A-H,O-Z), INTEGER*4 (I-N)
      PARAMETER (PI=3.1415926535897932D0)
      PARAMETER (A0B=5.291772108D-9)  ! Bohr radius (cm)
      PARAMETER (FPIAB2=4.0D0*PI*A0B**2)  ! (cm**2)
      PARAMETER (REV=5.10998918D5)  ! Electron rest energy (eV)
C
      DIMENSION UIS(99,9)  ! Dirac-Fock-Slater ionization energies.
      DIMENSION A(99,9,5)  ! Parameters.
      DIMENSION BE(99,9),ANLJ(99,9),G(99,9,4)
      DATA ((A(01,I,J),J=1,5),I=1,9)/
     1   1.381E+0, 4.611E-3,-1.417E+0, 1.481E+0,-1.306E+0, 40*0.0E+0/
      DATA (BE(01,I),ANLJ(01,I),(G(01,I,J),J=1,4),I=1,9)/
     1   1.513E+0, 1.509E-5, 4.882E-3, 1.426E+1,-3.163E-2, 2.426E-2,
     2   48*0.0E+0/
      DATA ((A(02,I,J),J=1,5),I=1,9)/
     1   1.113E+0, 4.781E-3,-1.483E+0, 1.495E+0,-2.124E+0, 40*0.0E+0/
      DATA (BE(02,I),ANLJ(02,I),(G(02,I,J),J=1,4),I=1,9)/
     1   1.331E+0, 2.567E-5, 4.821E-3, 1.143E+1,-2.959E-2, 2.160E-2,
     2   48*0.0E+0/
      DATA ((A(03,I,J),J=1,5),I=1,9)/
     1   4.825E-1, 2.164E-3,-7.372E-1, 9.963E-1,-2.412E+0, 40*0.0E+0/
      DATA (BE(03,I),ANLJ(03,I),(G(03,I,J),J=1,4),I=1,9)/
     1   1.253E+0, 1.304E-5, 6.617E-3, 9.888E+0,-3.302E-2, 2.482E-2,
     2   48*0.0E+0/
      DATA ((A(04,I,J),J=1,5),I=1,9)/
     1   2.468E-1, 1.177E-3,-3.540E-1, 3.895E-1,-5.390E-1, 40*0.0E+0/
      DATA (BE(04,I),ANLJ(04,I),(G(04,I,J),J=1,4),I=1,9)/
     1   1.206E+0, 6.679E-6, 9.973E-3, 9.308E+0,-4.437E-2, 3.308E-2,
     2   48*0.0E+0/
      DATA ((A(05,I,J),J=1,5),I=1,9)/
     1   1.488E-1, 7.157E-4,-2.091E-1, 2.234E-1,-3.021E-1, 40*0.0E+0/
      DATA (BE(05,I),ANLJ(05,I),(G(05,I,J),J=1,4),I=1,9)/
     1   1.210E+0, 3.932E-6, 1.366E-2, 8.912E+0,-5.541E-2, 3.989E-2,
     2   48*0.0E+0/
      DATA ((A(06,I,J),J=1,5),I=1,9)/
     1   9.994E-2, 4.881E-4,-1.391E-1, 1.487E-1,-2.024E-1, 40*0.0E+0/
      DATA (BE(06,I),ANLJ(06,I),(G(06,I,J),J=1,4),I=1,9)/
     1   1.206E+0, 2.610E-6, 1.764E-2, 8.570E+0,-6.750E-2, 4.667E-2,
     2   48*0.0E+0/

     1  1.71812E+4,5.52159E+3,5.18219E+3,4.28907E+3,3.73627E+3,
     2  3.55410E+3/
      DATA (UIS(93,J), J=1,9)/1.19193E+5,2.24389E+4,2.17027E+4,
     1  1.76255E+4,5.71234E+3,5.36610E+3,4.42095E+3,3.85851E+3,
     2  3.66689E+3/
      DATA (UIS(94,J), J=1,9)/1.22347E+5,2.31262E+4,2.23768E+4,
     1  1.80754E+4,5.90763E+3,5.55453E+3,4.55467E+3,3.98252E+3,
     2  3.78109E+3/
      DATA (UIS(95,J), J=1,9)/1.25563E+5,2.38302E+4,2.30678E+4,
     1  1.85312E+4,6.10762E+3,5.74766E+3,4.69027E+3,4.10835E+3,
     2  3.89671E+3/
      DATA (UIS(96,J), J=1,9)/1.28845E+5,2.45519E+4,2.37765E+4,
     1  1.89931E+4,6.31280E+3,5.94594E+3,4.82805E+3,4.23629E+3,
     2  4.01406E+3/
      DATA (UIS(97,J), J=1,9)/1.32196E+5,2.52919E+4,2.45034E+4,
     1  1.94608E+4,6.52316E+3,6.14931E+3,4.96778E+3,4.36611E+3,
     2  4.13288E+3/
      DATA (UIS(98,J), J=1,9)/1.35613E+5,2.60501E+4,2.52489E+4,
     1  1.99344E+4,6.73870E+3,6.35791E+3,5.10949E+3,4.49784E+3,
     2  4.25319E+3/
      DATA (UIS(99,J), J=1,9)/1.39103E+5,2.68279E+4,2.60139E+4,
     1  2.04140E+4,6.95977E+3,6.57198E+3,5.25320E+3,4.63150E+3,
     2  4.37501E+3/
C
      XIONE=0.0D0
      IF(IZ.LT.1.OR.IZ.GT.99) THEN
        WRITE(6,1001) IZ
 1001   FORMAT(1X,'STOP: The element IZ = ',I6,' is not available.',
     1    /1X,'Allowed atomic numbers range from 1 to 99.')
        STOP
      ENDIF
      IF(ISH.GT.9) THEN
        WRITE(6,1002) ISH
 1002   FORMAT(1X,'STOP: The shell ',I6,' is not available.',
     1    /1X,'Only K, L and M shells are parameterized.')
        STOP
      ENDIF
      UEV=UIS(IZ,ISH)
      IF(UEV.LT.1.0D-35) THEN
        WRITE(6,1003) ISH
 1003   FORMAT(1X,'STOP: The shell ',I6,' is not available for this',
     1    1X,'element. ')
        STOP
      ENDIF
      IF(EEV.LT.UEV) RETURN
      OVERV=EEV/UEV
      IF(OVERV.LE.16.0D0) THEN
        FFITLO=A(IZ,ISH,1)
     1        +A(IZ,ISH,2)*OVERV
     2        +A(IZ,ISH,3)/(1.0D0+OVERV)
     3        +A(IZ,ISH,4)/(1.0D0+OVERV)**3
     4        +A(IZ,ISH,5)/(1.0D0+OVERV)**5
        XIONE=((OVERV-1.0D0)/OVERV**2)*FFITLO**2
      ELSE IF(OVERV.GT.16.0D0) THEN
        BETA2=(EEV*(EEV+2.0D0*REV))/(EEV+REV)**2
        X=SQRT(EEV*(EEV+2.0D0*REV))/REV
        FFITUP=(2.0D0*LOG(X)-BETA2)*(1.0D0+G(IZ,ISH,1)/X)
     1        +G(IZ,ISH,2)
     2        +G(IZ,ISH,3)*(REV**2/(EEV+REV)**2)**(1.0D0/4.0D0)
     3        +G(IZ,ISH,4)/X
        FACTR=ANLJ(IZ,ISH)/BETA2
        XIONE=(FACTR*OVERV/(OVERV+BE(IZ,ISH)))*FFITUP
      ENDIF
      XIONE=FPIAB2*XIONE
C
      RETURN
      END
C  *********************************************************************
C                       FUNCION XIONP
C  *********************************************************************
      FUNCTION XIONP(EEV,IZ,ISH)
C
C     This function delivers the total cross section for positron impact
C  ionization of K, L and M shells of neutral atoms of the elements from
C  hydrogen (IZ=1) to einsteinium (IZ=99). It uses a parameterization of
C  numerical cross sections computed with the distorted-wave and the
C  plane-wave first-Born approximations.
C
C  References:
C  - D. Bote and F. Salvat, "Calculations of inner-shell ionization by
C       electron impact with the distorted-wave and plane-wave Born
C       approximations", Phys. Rev. A77, 042701 (2008).
C  - D. Bote et al., "Cross sections for ionization of K, L and M shells
C       of atoms by impact of electrons and positrons with energies up
C       to 1 GeV. Analytical formulas", At. and Nucl. Data Tables
C       95(6), 871--909 (2009).
C
C  Input Arguments:
C     EEV ..... kinetic energy of the projectile electron (in eV).
C     IZ ...... atomic number of the target atom (IZ=1 to 99).
C     ISH ..... active target electron shell,
C                1=K, 2=L1, 3=L2, 4=L3, 5=M1, ..., 9=M5.
C
C  Output value:
C     XIONP ... ionization cross section (in cm**2) of the ISH shell.
C
C  D. Bote, F. Salvat, A. Jablonski and C.J. Powell (November 2008)
C
      IMPLICIT DOUBLE PRECISION (A-H,O-Z), INTEGER*4 (I-N)
      PARAMETER (PI=3.1415926535897932D0)
      PARAMETER (A0B=5.291772108D-9)  ! Bohr radius (cm)
      PARAMETER (FPIAB2=4.0D0*PI*A0B**2)  ! (cm**2)
      PARAMETER (REV=5.10998918D5)  ! Electron rest energy (eV)
C
      DIMENSION UIS(99,9)  ! Dirac-Fock-Slater ionization energies.
      DIMENSION D(99,9,5)  ! Parameters.
      DIMENSION BP(99,9),ANLJ(99,9),G(99,9,4)
      DATA ((D(01,I,J),J=1,5),I=1,9)/
     1   1.075E+0, 5.977E-3, 6.653E-1,-1.255E+1, 1.222E+1, 40*0.0E+0/
      DATA (BP(01,I),ANLJ(01,I),(G(01,I,J),J=1,4),I=1,9)/
     1  -5.756E-2, 1.509E-5, 4.882E-3, 1.426E+1,-3.163E-2, 2.426E-2,
     2   48*0.0E+0/
      DATA ((D(02,I,J),J=1,5),I=1,9)/

      DATA ((D(05,I,J),J=1,5),I=1,9)/

     1  1.42147E+4,4.28614E+3,3.99255E+3,3.39827E+3,2.91119E+3,
     2  2.78549E+3/
      DATA (UIS(86,J), J=1,9)/9.87595E+4,1.80426E+4,1.73975E+4,
     1  1.46192E+4,4.44855E+3,4.14868E+3,3.51797E+3,3.02167E+3,
     2  2.88888E+3/
      DATA (UIS(87,J), J=1,9)/1.01513E+5,1.86303E+4,1.79724E+4,
     1  1.50344E+4,4.61993E+3,4.31361E+3,3.64454E+3,3.13898E+3,
     2  2.99878E+3/
      DATA (UIS(88,J), J=1,9)/1.04321E+5,1.92324E+4,1.85616E+4,
     1  1.54560E+4,4.79594E+3,4.48313E+3,3.77369E+3,3.25880E+3,
     2  3.11087E+3/
      DATA (UIS(89,J), J=1,9)/1.07184E+5,1.98478E+4,1.91640E+4,
     1  1.58824E+4,4.97507E+3,4.65566E+3,3.90375E+3,3.37946E+3,
     2  3.22349E+3/
      DATA (UIS(90,J), J=1,9)/1.10098E+5,2.04728E+4,1.97761E+4,
     1  1.63098E+4,5.15320E+3,4.82720E+3,4.03058E+3,3.49685E+3,
     2  3.33250E+3/
      DATA (UIS(91,J), J=1,9)/1.13071E+5,2.11129E+4,2.04029E+4,
     1  1.67427E+4,5.33535E+3,5.00263E+3,4.15897E+3,3.61574E+3,
     2  3.44266E+3/
      DATA (UIS(92,J), J=1,9)/1.16100E+5,2.17678E+4,2.10449E+4,
     1  1.71812E+4,5.52159E+3,5.18219E+3,4.28907E+3,3.73627E+3,
     2  3.55410E+3/
      DATA (UIS(93,J), J=1,9)/1.19193E+5,2.24389E+4,2.17027E+4,
     1  1.76255E+4,5.71234E+3,5.36610E+3,4.42095E+3,3.85851E+3,
     2  3.66689E+3/
      DATA (UIS(94,J), J=1,9)/1.22347E+5,2.31262E+4,2.23768E+4,
     1  1.80754E+4,5.90763E+3,5.55453E+3,4.55467E+3,3.98252E+3,
     2  3.78109E+3/
      DATA (UIS(95,J), J=1,9)/1.25563E+5,2.38302E+4,2.30678E+4,
     1  1.85312E+4,6.10762E+3,5.74766E+3,4.69027E+3,4.10835E+3,
     2  3.89671E+3/
      DATA (UIS(96,J), J=1,9)/1.28845E+5,2.45519E+4,2.37765E+4,
     1  1.89931E+4,6.31280E+3,5.94594E+3,4.82805E+3,4.23629E+3,
     2  4.01406E+3/
      DATA (UIS(97,J), J=1,9)/1.32196E+5,2.52919E+4,2.45034E+4,
     1  1.94608E+4,6.52316E+3,6.14931E+3,4.96778E+3,4.36611E+3,
     2  4.13288E+3/
      DATA (UIS(98,J), J=1,9)/1.35613E+5,2.60501E+4,2.52489E+4,
     1  1.99344E+4,6.73870E+3,6.35791E+3,5.10949E+3,4.49784E+3,
     2  4.25319E+3/
      DATA (UIS(99,J), J=1,9)/1.39103E+5,2.68279E+4,2.60139E+4,
     1  2.04140E+4,6.95977E+3,6.57198E+3,5.25320E+3,4.63150E+3,
     2  4.37501E+3/
C
      XIONP=0.0D0
      IF(IZ.LT.1.OR.IZ.GT.99) THEN
        WRITE(6,1001) IZ
 1001   FORMAT(1X,'STOP: The element IZ = ',I6,' is not available.',
     1    /1X,'Allowed atomic numbers range from 1 to 99.')
        STOP
      ENDIF
      IF(ISH.GT.9) THEN
        WRITE(6,1002) ISH
 1002   FORMAT(1X,'STOP: The shell ',I6,' is not available.',
     1    /1X,'Only K, L and M shells are parameterized.')
        STOP
      ENDIF
      UEV=UIS(IZ,ISH)
      IF(UEV.LT.1.0D-35) THEN
        WRITE(6,1003) ISH
 1003   FORMAT(1X,'STOP: The shell ',I6,' is not available for this',
     1    1X,'element. ')
        STOP
      ENDIF
      IF(EEV.LT.UEV) RETURN
      OVERV=EEV/UEV
      IF(OVERV.LE.16.0D0) THEN
        FFITLO=D(IZ,ISH,1)
     1        +D(IZ,ISH,2)*OVERV
     2        +D(IZ,ISH,3)/(1.0D0+OVERV)
     3        +D(IZ,ISH,4)*SQRT(OVERV)/(1.0D0+OVERV)**3
     4        +D(IZ,ISH,5)*OVERV/(1.0D0+OVERV)**6
        XIONP=((OVERV-1.0D0)/OVERV**2)*FFITLO**4
      ELSE IF(OVERV.GT.16.0D0) THEN
        BETA2=(EEV*(EEV+2.0D0*REV))/(EEV+REV)**2
        X=SQRT(EEV*(EEV+2.0D0*REV))/REV
        FFITUP=(2.0D0*LOG(X)-BETA2)*(1.0D0+G(IZ,ISH,1)/X)
     1        +G(IZ,ISH,2)
     2        +G(IZ,ISH,3)*(REV**2/(EEV+REV)**2)**(1.0D0/4.0D0)
     3        +G(IZ,ISH,4)/X
        FACTR=ANLJ(IZ,ISH)/BETA2
        XIONP=(FACTR*OVERV/(OVERV+BP(IZ,ISH)))*FFITUP
      ENDIF
      XIONP=FPIAB2*XIONP
C
      RETURN
      END
